## realestate.lead

Lead events


#### realestate.lead subscriptions receive

| Event | Description |
| :---- | :---------- |
| [realestate/lead#add](/messages#leadadd) | a crm lead was created |
| [realestate/lead#update](/messages#leadupdate) | a crm lead was updated |
| [realestate/lead#asssign](/messages#leadasssign) | a lead was assigned |
| [realestate/lead#accept](/messages#leadaccept) | a lead (object) was accepted by the agent |
| [realestate/lead#reject](/messages#leadreject) | a crm lead was accepted |
